Source: fileciteturn0file0 ## Current project state The chat continued development of `chatgpt_claudecode_workflow` / Promptbranch from **v0.0.149 through v0.0.175**, with **v0.0.176 started but not completed** in the transcript. **Latest accepted baseline:** ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.175.zip ``` **Do not assume v0.0.176 is accepted.** The transcript ends during implementation/testing of v0.0.176, before a final release artifact or validation summary was produced. ## Core architecture decisions carried forward Promptbranch is being developed as a constrained Claude-Code-like shell around ChatGPT Projects: ```text Promptbranch CLI / local host = control plane ChatGPT Project = workspace ChatGPT chat = task/session Sources / ZIPs = repo snapshots and release artifacts MCP = deterministic local tools Ollama = optional proposal/summarization only Skills = validated workflow instructions ``` Hard rules maintained throughout: ```text - Backend-first reads. - Transactional writes only. - State updates only after verified persistence. - Ollama never executes or chooses write actions. - Source/artifact writes stay gated until verified. - Release ZIPs must preserve baseline continuity. - ZIP root must contain repo contents directly, no wrapper folder. - Exclude .pytest_cache/, __pycache__/, *.pyc, logs, nested ZIPs, local state. ``` ## Release progression summary ### v0.0.150 Cleanup release from v0.0.149. Changed controlled terminology from “controlled writes” to: ```bash --include-controlled-processes ``` Controlled-process manifest exposes only: ```text test.smoke ``` Blocked: ```text promptbranch.src.sync artifact.release.create ``` Also fixed timeout diagnostics by separating tool timeout and transport timeout. ### v0.0.151 Diagnostics and packaging hygiene. Fixed brittle `mcp_host_smoke` behavior so it no longer tries: ```text filesystem.read "." ``` when `VERSION` / `README.md` is missing. Added git-root-aware skill path resolution. Added packaging regression coverage for: ```text .pytest_cache/ __pycache__/ *.pyc ``` ### v0.0.152 Added safe log summarization: ```bash pb agent summarize-log <log-file> --path . --json ``` Properties: ```text repo-bounded read-only bounded max bytes Ollama used only for summary no tool execution no state mutation ``` Also fixed duplicate JSON output from agent commands. ### v0.0.153 Added deterministic fallback summary when Ollama times out or is unavailable. Instead of failing only as `summary_unavailable`, `summarize-log` can return: ```text deterministic_summary ``` with local heuristic counts and failure markers. ### v0.0.154 Added test-suite profiles: ```bash pb test-suite --profile browser --json pb test-suite --profile agent --json pb test-suite --profile full --json ``` Agent profile includes MCP host-smoke, skill validation, controlled smoke process, summarize-log, negative safety checks, and package hygiene. ### v0.0.155 Added canonical shortcut commands: ```bash pb test browser --json pb test agent --json pb test full --json ``` These map to the profile system from v0.0.154. ### v0.0.156 Made full test profile rate-limit-safe by default after real ChatGPT 429/conversation-history throttling appeared. Added: ```bash pb test full --rate-limit-safe --json pb test full --no-rate-limit-safe --json ``` ### v0.0.157 Added rate-limit telemetry into full test-suite JSON output. Telemetry tracks planned cooldowns, actual cooldowns, modal detection, and conversation-history 429s. ### v0.0.158 Added: ```bash pb test report <log> --json ``` It parses noisy full-suite logs and extracts browser/agent failures, telemetry, package hygiene, safety state, and optional service-log evidence. ### v0.0.159 Fixed packaging regression from v0.0.158. Root cause: `promptbranch_cli.py` imported `promptbranch_test_report`, but that module was missing from `pyproject.toml` `py-modules`. v0.0.159 added the module and regression coverage. ### v0.0.160 Added installed-package import smoke check: ```bash pb test import-smoke --json ``` Purpose: catch missing installed modules from outside the source tree, so local files cannot mask packaging metadata errors. ### v0.0.161 Added: ```bash pb test status --json ``` Reports newest valid full-suite status without rerunning browser automation. ### v0.0.162 Fixed JSON stdout cleanliness. Problem: DEBUG/logging noise could appear before JSON, breaking: ```bash pb test status --json | python3 -m json.tool ``` Fix: quiet-by-default logging for JSON mode unless `--debug` is explicitly used. ### v0.0.163 Fixed status/report log selection issues. Problem: invalid or tiny logs could be skipped, causing `pb test status` to fall back to older valid logs and hide the newest failure. v0.0.163 tightened newest-log handling and invalid-log reporting. ### v0.0.164 Fixed report/status robustness after a rerun exposed parse issues. The full suite itself passed, but report/status handling needed better behavior around malformed/noisy logs. ### v0.0.165 Added runtime/release version consistency checks. Checks include: ```text VERSION pyproject/package version promptbranch version output MCP server version container/service version report/test-suite version surfaces ``` ### v0.0.166 Shifted back toward MVP source-sync work. Added non-mutating source sync plan: ```bash pb src sync . --dry-run --json pb src sync . --plan --json ``` No ZIP creation, no registry update, no upload, no state mutation. ### v0.0.167 Enhanced source-sync dry-run with transaction metadata: ```text transaction_id before_snapshot collateral_checks verification_plan git/worktree snapshot artifact registry snapshot excluded file count/sample collision checks ``` Still non-mutating. ### v0.0.168 Added verified local source-sync packaging: ```bash pb src sync . --no-upload --json ``` Success status: ```text verified_packaged ``` It writes a local ZIP, verifies integrity/SHA, updates local artifact registry/state, and confirms no ChatGPT Project source mutation occurred. Collision safety added; overwrite requires: ```bash --force ``` ### v0.0.169 Removed ambiguous default mutation behavior. Now: ```bash pb src sync . --json ``` refuses with: ```text sync_mode_required ``` Operator must choose: ```bash --no-upload ``` or: ```bash --upload ``` `--upload --json` is preflight only and returns `upload_confirmation_required`. ### v0.0.170 Live upload confirmation now requires a transaction ID. Preflight returns: ```text transaction_id confirm_command ``` Confirmed upload must include: ```bash --confirm-upload --confirm-transaction-id <id> ``` Without ID, it refuses: ```text upload_transaction_id_required ``` ### v0.0.171 Deferred local artifact registry/source state advancement until project upload verifies. Rule established: ```text Local ZIP may be written. Registry/source state advances only after verified upload. Failed upload must not advance registry/state. ``` ### v0.0.172 Improved upload preflight around local artifact collisions. If local artifact exists, preflight sets: ```text force_required: true ``` and generated confirm command includes: ```bash --force ``` Confirmed upload without required force refuses. ### v0.0.173 Made upload transaction ID content-bound. Added repo manifest fingerprint based on: ```text included path file size file SHA-256 ``` If repo content changes after preflight, confirm with old transaction ID refuses: ```text upload_transaction_id_mismatch ``` ### v0.0.174 Added source-list verification after confirmed upload. Confirmed upload now requires: ```text upload_result.ok == true before source list readable after source list readable expected ZIP filename present after upload no collateral source removals detected ``` Only then should registry/state advance. ### v0.0.175 Fixed confirmed-upload crash. Real live upload produced a service error: ```text 504 error for POST /v1/project-sources Could not find the remove/delete action for the selected project source ``` v0.0.174 crashed with traceback. v0.0.175 catches service errors and returns structured JSON: ```text status: upload_failed artifact_registry_updated: false state_source_updated: false project_source_mutated: false ``` ## Latest discovered issue After v0.0.175, a live confirmed upload returned internally inconsistent evidence: ```text upload_result.status: service_error http_status_code: 504 ``` but after-snapshot showed the expected uploaded ZIP present: ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.175.zip matching_expected_count: 1 collateral_change_detected: false ``` Interpretation: possible partial/ambiguous success. The service errored, but source-list verification saw the expected file. Correct next behavior should be: ```text status: upload_ambiguous expected_source_present_after: true upload_result_ok: false artifact_registry_updated: false state_source_updated: false operator_review_required: true ``` ## v0.0.176 status v0.0.176 was started from: ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.175.zip ``` Intended scope: ```text - classify upload-result/source-list disagreement as upload_ambiguous - keep registry/state unadvanced - require operator review - preserve ZIP hygiene - update all version surfaces ``` But the transcript ends during implementation/testing, around modifications to `promptbranch_cli.py` and tests. Detect disagreement: - upload_result.ok == false - expected source appears after upload - no collateral removal 3. Return operator_review_required: true. 4. Do not update artifact registry. 5. _find_project_source_container(self, page: Any, source_name: str, *, exact: bool) -> Optional[Any]:\n''' helper=r''' async def _find_project_source_remove_action(self, page: Any) -> Optional[Any]: """Find a visible source remove/delete menu action using broad DOM fallback. ChatGPT's project source menu markup changes over time. Some builds render menu actions as role=menuitem; others render generic div/span/button items inside a floating menu. This fallback is used only after the source row's options button was clicked and selector-based lookup failed. """ try: handle = await page.evaluate_handle( r""" () => { const normalize = value => (value || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim(); const normalizeLower = value => normalize(value).toLowerCase(); const isVisible = el => { if (!el || !el.getBoundingClientRect) return false; const style = window.getComputedStyle(el); if (!style || style.display === 'none' || style.visibility === 'hidden' || style.pointerEvents === 'none') return false; const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect(); return rect.width > 0 && rect.height > 0 && rect.bottom >= 0 && rect.top <= window.innerHeight; }; const actionText = el => normalize( el.innerText || el.textContent || el.getAttribute('aria-label') || el.getAttribute('title') || el.getAttribute('data-testid') || '' ); const looksLikeMenuSurface = el => !!( el && el.closest && el.closest( '[role="menu"], [role="listbox"], [data-radix-popper-content-wrapper], [data-floating-ui-portal], [cmdk-list], [data-headlessui-portal], [role="dialog"]' ) ); const isRemoveCandidate = el => { if (!isVisible(el)) return false; const label = normalizeLower(actionText(el)); if (!label) return false; if (label.includes('project') || label.includes('conversation') || label.includes('chat')) return false; if (label === 'remove' || label === 'delete') return true; if (label === 'remove source' || label === 'delete source') return true; if (label === 'remove file' || label === 'delete file') return true; if (label.includes('remove from project')) return true; if (label.includes('delete from project')) return true; if ((label.includes('remove') || label.includes('delete')) && (label.includes('source') || label.includes('file') || label.includes('document'))) return true; return false; }; const selectors = [ '[role="menuitem"]', '[role="option"]', '[cmdk-item]', '[data-radix-collection-item]', 'button', '[role="button"]', 'a', 'div', 'span' ]; const nodes = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(selectors.join(','))).filter(isVisible); const scored = []; for (const node of nodes) { if (!isRemoveCandidate(node)) continue; const label = normalizeLower(actionText(node)); const role = normalizeLower(node.getAttribute('role') || ''); const tag = normalizeLower(node.tagName || ''); let score = 0; if (looksLikeMenuSurface(node)) score += 100; if (role === 'menuitem') score += 80; if (tag === 'button') score += 60; if (label === 'remove' || label === 'delete') score += 40; if (label.includes('source') || label.includes('file')) score += 20; bash -lc cat > /mnt/data/chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_release_control.sh <<'EOF' #!/usr/bin/env bash set -Eeuo pipefail # ChatGPT Claude Code Workflow release ZIP / compare / commit / install / source-control workflow. # Run from the repository root: /home/spikkie/git/chatgpt_claudecode_workflow # # Version precedence, highest first: # 1. --version / -v / first positional argument # 2. PB_RELEASE_VERSION environment variable # 3. VERSION file in the repo root # # Version examples accepted: # v0.0.184 # 0.0.184 # chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.184.zip # # This script intentionally uses real commands instead of shell aliases: # bc -> bcompare # ga -> git add . # gcm -> git commit -m ... # gp -> git push # zip_it -> ~/scripts/zip_with_not_to_zip.sh, with a Python fallback # pbsa -> promptbranch src add ... project_name="chatgpt_claudecode_workflow" repo_root="$(pwd)" version_file="${repo_root}/VERSION" downloads_dir="${DOWNLOADS_DIR:-${HOME}/Downloads}" work_parent="${TMPDIR:-/tmp}/${project_name}_release_import" container_id="${PROMPTBRANCH_CONTAINER_ID:-}" owner_user="${PROMPTBRANCH_OWNER_USER:-${SUDO_USER:-${USER}}}" owner_group="${PROMPTBRANCH_OWNER_GROUP:-${owner_user}}" version_arg="${PB_RELEASE_VERSION:-}" skip_compare=0 skip_commit=0 skip_push=0 skip_source_add=0 skip_install=0 skip_chown=0 skip_service=0 skip_tests=0 skip_docker_logs=0 keep_workdir=0 default_packager="${HOME}/scripts/zip_with_not_to_zip.sh" packager="${PROMPTBRANCH_PACKAGER:-${default_packager}}" usage() { cat <<USAGE Usage: $(basename "$0") --version v0.0.184 [options] $(basename "$0") v0.0.184 [options] Options: -v, --version VERSION Highest-precedence release version override. Accepts v0.0.184, 0.0.184, or ${project_name}_v0.0.184.zip. --downloads-dir DIR Directory containing the downloaded baseline ZIP. Default: ~/Downloads. --container-id ID Docker container id/name for service logs. Auto-detected if omitted. --owner USER[:GROUP] Owner for .pb_profile after install. Default: ${owner_user}:${owner_group}. --packager PATH Packaging helper. Default: ${default_packager}. --skip-compare Skip Beyond Compare import comparison. --skip-commit Skip git add/commit/push. --no-push Commit but do not git push. --skip-source-add Skip promptbranch src add. --skip-install Skip pipx reinstall from generated ZIP. --skip-chown Skip chown of .pb_profile. --skip-service Skip ./run_chatgpt_service.sh. --skip-tests Skip pb test full/report. --skip-docker-logs Skip docker logs capture. --keep-workdir Keep temporary extracted comparison directory. -h, --help Show this help. Version precedence: CLI argument > PB_RELEASE_VERSION > VERSION file Typical use: $(basename "$0") --version v0.0.184 USAGE } fail() { echo "ERROR: $*" >&2 exit 1 } need_cmd() { command -v "$1" >/dev/null 2>&1 || fail "$1 is required" } normalize_version() { local raw="$1" raw="${raw##*/}" raw="${raw%.zip}" raw="${raw#${project_name}_}" raw="${raw#${project_name}}" raw="${raw#_}" if [[ "${raw}" =~ ^v?[0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then raw="${raw#v}" printf 'v%s\n' "${raw}" return 0 fi return 1 } while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do case "$1" in -v|--version) [[ $# -ge 2 ]] || fail "--version requires a value" version_arg="$2" shift 2 ;; --version=*) version_arg="${1#*=}" shift ;; --downloads-dir) [[ $# -ge 2 ]] || fail "--downloads-dir requires a value" downloads_dir="$2" shift 2 ;; --downloads-dir=*) downloads_dir="${1#*=}" shift ;; --container-id) [[ $# -ge 2 ]] || fail "--container-id requires a value" container_id="$2" shift 2 ;; --container-id=*) container_id="${1#*=}" shift ;; --owner) [[ $# -ge 2 ]] || fail "--owner requires USER or USER:GROUP" owner_user="${2%%:*}" owner_group="${2#*:}" [[ "${owner_group}" != "${2}" ]] || owner_group="${owner_user}" shift 2 ;; --owner=*) owner_value="${1#*=}" owner_user="${owner_value%%:*}" owner_group="${owner_value#*:}" [[ "${owner_group}" != "${owner_value}" ]] || owner_group="${owner_user}" shift ;; --packager) [[ $# -ge 2 ]] || fail "--packager requires a path" packager="$2" shift 2 ;; --packager=*) packager="${1#*=}" shift ;; --skip-compare) skip_compare=1; shift ;; --skip-commit) skip_commit=1; shift ;; --no-push) skip_push=1; shift ;; --skip-source-add) skip_source_add=1; shift ;; --skip-install) skip_install=1; shift ;; --skip-chown) skip_chown=1; shift ;; --skip-service) skip_service=1; shift ;; --skip-tests) skip_tests=1; shift ;; --skip-docker-logs) skip_docker_logs=1; shift ;; --keep-workdir) keep_workdir=1; shift ;; -h|--help) usage; exit 0 ;; --*) fail "unknown option: $1" ;; *) if [[ -z "${version_arg}" ]]; then version_arg="$1" shift else fail "unexpected positional argument: $1" fi ;; esac done if [[ -z "${version_arg}" ]]; then [[ -f "${version_file}" ]] || fail "VERSION file not found and no --version supplied: ${version_file}" version_arg="$(head -n 1 "${version_file}" | tr -d '[:space:]')" fi ver="$(normalize_version "${version_arg}")" || fail "version must look like v0.0.184, 0.0.184, or ${project_name}_v0.0.184.zip; got '${version_arg}'" ver_plain="${ver#v}" artifact_zip="${project_name}_${ver}.zip" download_zip="${downloads_dir}/${artifact_zip}" work_dir="${work_parent}/${project_name}_${ver}" full_log="pb_test.full.${ver}.log" report_json="pb_test.full.${ver}.report.json" service_log="promptbranch-service:${ver_plain}.log" if [[ ! -f "${download_zip}" ]]; then fail "Download ZIP not found: ${download_zip}" fi need_cmd unzip need_cmd git need_cmd python3 need_cmd pipx need_cmd promptbranch if [[ ${skip_compare} -eq 0 ]]; then need_cmd bcompare fi if [[ ${skip_docker_logs} -eq 0 ]]; then need_cmd docker fi printf '\n== Release control ==\n' printf 'repo_root: %s\n' "${repo_root}" printf 'version: %s\n' "${ver}" printf 'artifact_zip: %s\n' "${artifact_zip}" printf 'download_zip: %s\n' "${download_zip}" printf 'work_dir: %s\n' "${work_dir}" printf '\n' # Import downloaded baseline ZIP into a temporary directory and visually compare it to the repo. rm -rf "${work_dir}" mkdir -p "${work_dir}" cp "${download_zip}" "${work_dir}/${artifact_zip}" ( cd "${work_dir}" unzip -q "${artifact_zip}" rm -f "${artifact_zip}" ) if [[ ${skip_compare} -eq 0 ]]; then # Beyond Compare may return non-zero for differences; differences are the point here. bcompare "${work_dir}" "${repo_root}" || true fi if [[ ${keep_workdir} -eq 0 ]]; then rm -rf "${work_dir}" fi # Commit current working tree with the release ZIP name as commit message. if [[ ${skip_commit} -eq 0 ]]; then git add . if git diff --cached --quiet; then echo "No staged git changes; skipping git commit." else git commit -m "${artifact_zip}" fi if [[ ${skip_push} -eq 0 ]]; then git push fi fi # Build canonical release ZIP. Prefer your existing packager, but provide a strict fallback. if [[ -x "${packager}" ]]; then "${packager}" else echo "WARN: packager not executable: ${packager}" echo "WARN: using built-in Python packaging fallback." python3 - "${repo_root}" "${artifact_zip}" <<'PY' from pathlib import Path import fnmatch import os import sys import zipfile root = Path(sys.argv[1]).resolve() out = root / sys.argv[2] exclude_patterns = [ ".git/", "__pycache__/", "*.pyc", "*.pyo", ".pytest_cache/", ".mypy_cache/", ".ruff_cache/", "node_modules/", "dist/", "build/", "coverage/", ".venv/", "venv/", "env/", ".env", ".env.*", "*.zip", "*.tar.gz", "*.log", ".pb_profile/", "profile/", "debug_artifacts/", ".DS_Store", ] not_to_zip = root / ".not_to_zip" if not_to_zip.exists(): for line in not_to_zip.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace").splitlines(): line = line.strip() if not line or line.startswith("#") or line.startswith("!"): continue exclude_patterns.append(line) def match(rel: str, pattern: str, is_dir: bool) -> bool: rel = rel.strip("/") pattern = pattern.strip() if not pattern: return False directory_only = pattern.endswith("/") pattern = pattern.strip("/") if directory_only and not is_dir and not rel.startswith(pattern + "/"): return False candidates = {rel, Path(rel).name} if is_dir: candidates.add(rel + "/") return any(fnmatch.fnmatch(candidate, pattern) for candidate in candidates) or fnmatch.fnmatch(rel, pattern) or rel.startswith(pattern + "/") def excluded(path: Path) -> bool: rel = path.relative_to(root).as_posix() if any(part in {".git", "__pycache__", ".pytest_cache"} for part in rel.split("/")): return True if path.suffix in {".pyc", ".pyo"}: return True parts = rel.split("/") for i in range(1, len(parts) + 1): candidate = "/".join(parts[:i]) candidate_path = root / candidate is_dir = i < len(parts) or candidate_path.is_dir() if any(match(candidate, pattern, is_dir) for pattern in exclude_patterns): return True return False files = [] for current, dirs, filenames in os.walk(root): current_path = Path(current) dirs[:] = [d for d in sorted(dirs) if not excluded(current_path / d)] for filename in sorted(filenames): path = current_path / filename if path == out: continue if not excluded(path): files.append(path) if out.exists(): out.unlink() with zipfile.ZipFile(out, "w", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED, compresslevel=6) as archive: for path in sorted(files, key=lambda p: p.relative_to(root).as_posix()): archive.write(path, path.relative_to(root).as_posix()) print(f"created {out}") PY fi # Normalize possible packager output names to canonical artifact name. for candidate in \ "source_${ver}.zip" \ "source_${ver_plain}.zip" \ "source_${project_name}_${ver}.zip" \ "source_${project_name}_${ver_plain}.zip" \ "${project_name}_${ver}.zip" do if [[ -f "${candidate}" ]]; then if [[ "${candidate}" != "${artifact_zip}" ]]; then mv -f "${candidate}" "${artifact_zip}" fi break fi done [[ -f "${artifact_zip}" ]] || fail "could not find packaging output for version ${ver}; expected ${artifact_zip} or source_* variants" # Verify ZIP hygiene before using it. python3 - "${artifact_zip}" "${ver}" <<'PY' import sys import zipfile from pathlib import Path zip_path = Path(sys.argv[1]) expected_version = sys.argv[2] with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path) as z: bad_crc = z.testzip() if bad_crc: raise SystemExit(f"ZIP CRC failure at {bad_crc}") names = z.namelist() bad_entries = [n for n in names if ".pytest_cache" in n or "__pycache__" in n or n.endswith((".pyc", ".pyo"))] if bad_entries: raise SystemExit("bad generated/cache entries in ZIP: " + ", ".join(bad_entries[:20])) roots = {n.split("/")[0] for n in names if n.strip("/")} wrapper = len(roots) == 1 and all("/" in n for n in names if n.strip("/")) if wrapper: raise SystemExit("ZIP appears to contain a wrapper/root folder") version = z.read("VERSION").decode("utf-8").strip() if version != expected_version: raise SystemExit(f"VERSION mismatch in ZIP: expected {expected_version}, got {version}") print(f"ZIP verified: {zip_path}") PY # Add release ZIP to ChatGPT Project Sources. if [[ ${skip_source_add} -eq 0 ]]; then promptbranch src add "${artifact_zip}" fi # Reinstall local CLI from the release ZIP. if [[ ${skip_install} -eq 0 ]]; then pipx uninstall promptbranch || true pipx install "./${artifact_zip}" fi # Restore ownership of Promptbranch profile if needed. if [[ ${skip_chown} -eq 0 && -d "${repo_root}/.pb_profile" ]]; then sudo chown -R "${owner_user}:${owner_group}" "${repo_root}/.pb_profile/" fi # Start/restart ChatGPT service using repo script. if [[ ${skip_service} -eq 0 ]]; then [[ -x "./run_chatgpt_service.sh" ]] || fail "service script not executable: ./run_chatgpt_service.sh" ./run_chatgpt_service.sh fi # Run full suite and parsed report. if [[ ${skip_tests} -eq 0 ]]; then pb test full --json 2>&1 | tee "${full_log}" pb test report "${full_log}" --json | python3 -m json.tool | tee "${report_json}" fi # Capture service logs. if [[ ${skip_docker_logs} -eq 0 ]]; then if [[ -z "${container_id}" ]]; then container_id="$(docker ps --format '{{.ID}} {{.Image}} {{.Names}}' | awk '/promptbranch|chatgpt/ {print $1; exit}')" fi if [[ -z "${container_id}" ]]; then echo "WARN: no promptbranch/chatgpt docker container auto-detected; skipping docker logs" >&2 else docker logs "${container_id}" > "${service_log}" echo "Service log written: ${service_log}" fi fi cat <<DONE Release workflow completed. version: ${ver} artifact: ${artifact_zip} full_log: ${full_log} report_json: ${report_json} service_log: ${service_log} DONE EOF chmod +x /mnt/data/chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_release_control.sh ls -l Mandatory exclusions. for pat in [ '.git/','__pycache__/','*.pyc','*.pyo','.pytest_cache/','.mypy_cache/','.ruff_cache/', 'build/','dist/','.venv/','venv/','env/','node_modules/','.DS_Store', '*.log','*.tmp','*.bak','*.swp','*.zip','*.tar.gz','.pb_profile/','debug_artifacts/', 'chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v*/','profile/','coverage/', ]: add(pat) ntz=root/'.not_to_zip' if ntz.is_file(): for line in ntz.read_text(encoding='utf-8').splitlines(): add(line) def match(rel, pat, is_dir=False): rel=rel.strip('/') pat=pat.strip() if not pat: return False directory_only=pat.endswith('/') pat=pat.strip('/') if directory_only and not (is_dir or rel.startswith(pat + '/')): return False candidates={rel, Path(rel).name} if is_dir: candidates.add(rel + '/') return any(fnmatch.fnmatch(c, pat) for c in candidates) or fnmatch.fnmatch(rel, pat) or rel.startswith(pat + '/') def is_allowed(p): rel=p.relative_to(root).as_posix() return any(match(rel, pat, p.is_dir()) for pat in allow) def excluded(p): rel=p.relative_to(root).as_posix() parts=set(rel.split('/')) if parts & {'.git','__pycache__','.pytest_cache','.mypy_cache','.ruff_cache'}: return True if p.is_file() and (p.suffix in {'.pyc','.pyo'} or p.name.endswith('.log')): return True if is_allowed(p): return False # Use a fresh version number that is absent from Project Sources. Run pb src list --json first to confirm absence. Then run the artifact-release preflight/confirm. ``` ## For the current path For `v0.0.188`, do **not** manually add: ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.188.zip ``` before testing the upload transaction. ## Critical answer **`chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.188.zip` is created by the release build step, not by the upload confirmation step.** The automatic upload path does **not** invent the next version number. It packages whatever version the repo currently declares in `VERSION` and related metadata. Your log shows the problem clearly: you named the preflight output file as if you were testing `v0.0.188`: ```bash /tmp/promptbranch-upload/pb_artifact_release_preflight.v0.0.188.json ``` but Promptbranch actually planned this artifact: ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.187.zip version: v0.0.187 ``` So the repo was still at `v0.0.187`, not `v0.0.188`. fileciteturn68file0 ## Two different ZIP concepts ### 1. Release ZIP for installing Promptbranch This is the ZIP we build during development: ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.188.zip ``` This ZIP must be created by the **release build process** after bumping all version surfaces to `v0.0.188`. That means: ```text VERSION pyproject.toml promptbranch_version.py promptbranch_cli.py / version surfaces promptbranch_mcp.py promptbranch_container_api.py docker-compose.chatgpt-service.yml UPGRADING.md / README if needed tests expecting version ``` Then package the repo into: ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.188.zip ``` Then install it: ```bash pipx uninstall promptbranch pipx install ./chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.188.zip ``` ### 2. Project-source upload artifact This is created by: ```bash pb artifact release . --sync-source --upload --json ``` But it uses the **current repo version**. If `VERSION` says `v0.0.187`, it creates/plans: ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.187.zip ``` not `v0.0.188`. ## Why your test hit a collision Your Project Sources already had: ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.187.zip ``` The log shows it listed in Project Sources before the test. fileciteturn68file0 Then `pb artifact release` also planned `v0.0.187`, causing: ```text force_required: true local artifact collision ``` That is expected because you were not actually testing a fresh `v0.0.188`. ## Correct next step First we need to **build `v0.0.188`** from the accepted baseline. Current accepted baseline remains: ```text chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.185.zip ``` `v0.0.188` should include the fixes we identified: ```text 1. Top-level artifact-release confirm supports --force correctly. 2. No executable nested src_sync confirm command leaks to the operator. 3. .promptbranch-service-start.*.pid stays excluded. 4. Artifact-release confirm wrapper maps src_sync success to top-level status: uploaded. 5. Regression coverage for force / uploaded / failed / ambiguous wrapper outcomes. ``` After I build `chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.188.zip`, then you install it and test: ```bash pbv pb src list --json | python3 -m json.tool pb artifact release . --sync-source --upload --json \ | tee /tmp/promptbranch-upload/pb_artifact_release_preflight.v0.0.188.json \ | python3 -m json.tool ``` Then run only: ```text confirmation.confirm_command ``` ## Verdict ✅ `pb artifact release` creates the upload artifact, but only for the version currently in the repo. ⚠️ Your repo was still at `v0.0.187`, so it could not create `chatgpt_claudecode_workflow_v0.0.188.zip`. 🔍 The file name of the log/preflight JSON does not control the artifact version. 🧩 Next step — build the actual `v0.0.188` release ZIP first, then test automatic upload without manually adding that ZIP to Project Sources.
